(மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) Mr. Somawansa Amarasinghe. He says so, he claims so. He is a Britisher with a Sri Lankan passport. Has he not got dual citizenship? What is this hypocrisy that is there? When they outlaw them, හුෙර් කියනවා. When they interfere with the activities when there is a problem - when there are certain things that have got to be followed for the proscription, the former Minister of Foreign Affairs, the Hon. Mangala Samaraweera had to agree to certain conditions and when you breach them they have to come and investigate; දැන් චිෙක් කියනවා. One and a half or two years ago, was it not this same Parliament, the same party that gave accolade and said, yes, we appreciate the banning of the Tigers by the European Union? Is not the United Kingdom a part of that? Was that not because of the Ceasefire Agreement that the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe, the then Prime Minister signed? We had the Co-Chairs, were they not signatories? All of them unanimously said, yes, there is a breach and you need to ensure that there is a proscription imposed. So, Sir, this has to be looked at from different perspectives, different angles and not just with blinked eyes like an ostrich with its head in the sand. We, the United National Party has always been a responsible party. Today, the Hon. Mahinda Rajapaksa, the President of this country is having enormous problems. Our Leader was magnanimous enough to extend a lending hand in November 2006 to come up with an MoU. You said you have problems. You called us for help and we agreed. That is disregarded and then you blame the rest of the world. We are repeating that we do not want any foreign intervention in our country. That is very clear. But at the same time, we are a great believer that we require the international community to come to our assistance in our time of need. They can guide us. They can give their absolute assistance from their practical experiences. Now, I table* the Hansard of the British Parliament containing that particular debate which has seven pages in it. Sir, I want to ensure that this is printed in Hansard instead of just being placed in the library. When the Minister of Middle-East Affairs, Dr. Kim Howells started the Debate, he stated in reply to questions that came up as to why this Debate needs to take place. He said, “We have rich experience through the Northern Ireland process. The President of Sri Lanka had come to seek our assistance and we did extend our services.” So, on that basis the proscription took place. The Hon. Mangala Samaeraweera had to write and confirm that they will ensure the human rights and media

freedom would be guaranteed. I am sure the Minister of Foreign Affairs who will speak later on obviously will have a headache. He will be able to ensure and give light to this by saying, “Yes, there was a commitment.” The breach of that has given the opportunity for the international community to peep into Sri Lankan affairs. Who is held responsible for that? The Executive President of this country for the last 14 years has been from the Sri Lanka Freedom Party. They are the ones who have let this in. Their incompetency, their inaptness has led to such a situation and then they blame the rest of the world. වැඩ බැරි ටාසන්ලා ෙවලායි දැන් ඉන්ෙන්. අද එංගලන්තෙය් ෙපොල් ෙගඩියක් වැටුණත් - [බාධා කිරීමක්] වැඩ බැරි ටාසන්ලායි අද ෙම් ඉන්ෙන්. ෙමොනවාද, කියන්ෙන්? මා කියන්නම්. When there is a flood, when there is a shortage of general utilities in Sri Lanka, when the cost of living is zooming, when human rights are being violated, when media personnel are being harassed you put the blame on someone else. The general situation today is not reflected in issues in Colombo. They are reflected in issues overseas. As I said, Dr. Howells of the British Parliament has said, “Owing to our experience we are coming forward.” It is a friendly persuasion. This is not something dropped from the air. That is the difference here. Who has led this to a situation of foreign intervention? As you know, Sir, we are signatories to international treaties on Human Rights such as International Covenant on Civil and Political Rights monitored by the Human Rights Committee of 1980, then subsequently to the Optional Protocol to the International Covenant on Civil and Political Rights administered by the Human Rights Committee on 3rd January, 1998. These are the Covenants that bind Sri Lanka with the international community. There is no way that we can live in isolation. Ours is an island. We have got to ensure that we live with the world community. So with all these international agreements, when in 1983 the Janatha Vimukthi Peramuna attacked all the public properties creating mayhem in this country, it was proscribed and with the proscription the then leader of the Janatha Vimukthi Peramuna, Mr. Rohana Wijeweera said that there were incidents of human rights violations taking place and wanted the international community to look at Sri Lanka. Was that not the case? Then, likewise the then Member of the Opposition, the present President, the Hon. Mahinda Rajapaksa, quite rightly may be, in his perception he would have felt that there was a violation of human rights during the period 1988 to 1989 and he tried to take evidence to be produced before international fora, not legally but hidden inside his shoes. At that particular moment did he not bring that matter into international light and say there was a problem in the human rights situation? Today, the Parliamentary Leader of the Janatha Vimukthi Peramuna, the Hon. Wimal Weerawansa mentioned about Aung San Suu Kyi of Myanmar. An

* කථාව අවසානෙය් පළ කර ඇත. உைரயினிᾠதியில் தரப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ. Produced at end of speech.

Adjournment Motion was brought before this House sometime back. At that time Myanmar could have turned around and said, “What right have you got to discuss about Myanmar?” When the world famous Buddha statues of Bamian in Afghanistan were demolished by some barbarians there, we took that matter up in this House. They too could have turned around and said, “What has Sri Lanka got to do with this?” It is not so. When there is a problem that concerns the international community, these types of situations do come up. So, instead of trying to create problems, we have got to ensure that we attend to such problems in a friendly manner. You can catch more bees with honey than with vinegar, Sir. That is what we, the United National Party are saying. Going on further, I would also like to mention what the Deputy Solicitor General, Mr. Palitha Fernando said at a passing-out ceremony at the Police Academy just a couple of days ago. To save time I table* Annex 5. I will only read the important sections pertaining to this situation. It states, I quote:

"අෙප් රෙට් ඇතුළත තිෙබන පශ්නවලට ඇතුළත් ෙවන්න. ඒක ඉතාමත්ම පැහැදිලිව එක්සත් ජාතීන්ෙග් පඥප්තිෙය් සඳහන් කරල තිෙබනවා. නමුත්, එම යුද්ධය කරන අවස්ථාෙව් දී අපි අතින් මානව හිමිකම් කඩ වනවා නම් ඔවුන්ට පුළුවන් මැදිහත් ෙවන්න අෙප් රෙට් පශ්නවලට. අන්න ඒ අවස්ථාෙව් ඒ අභɕන්තර පශ්නය තවදුරටත් අභɕන්තර පශ්නයක් වන්ෙන් නැහැ. බාහිර පුද්ගලයන්ට; එක්සත් ජාතීන්ට පුළුවන් පශ්න කරන්න. 'ඇයි ඔබ රෙට් මානව හිමිකම් ෙමෙලස කඩ ෙවනවා නම් ඔබ ඒ සඳහා ගන්නා වූ පියවර කුමක් ද?' කියලා පශ්න කරන්න පුළුවන්. රාජɕ බලය කියාත්මක කරලා මානව හිමිකම් උල්ලංඝනය කෙළොත් යම් කිසි ෙකෙනක්, ඒ මානව හිමිකම් උල්ලංඝනය කිරීමට රජයත් වග කියන්න ඕනෑ. තමුන්නාන්ෙසේලා රාජකාරිය ඉටු කරන්න ආපු හැම අවස්ථාවකදී ම මානව හිමිකම් කඩ ෙනොවන ආකාරයට තමන්ෙග් රාජකාරි ඉටු කරන්න. එෙහම නැත්නම් මානව හිමිකම් කඩ ෙනොවන ආකාරයට තමුන්නාන්ෙසේලා රාජකාරිය ඉටු කරන්ෙන් නැත්නම්, රෙට් පතිරූපය ෙලෝකය ඉදිරිෙය් ෙකෙලෙසනවා විතරක් ෙනොෙව්, රෙට් අභɕන්තර පශ්නවලට මැදිහත් වීෙම් අයිතිය බාහිර බලෙව්ගයට ලබා ෙදනවා."

Deputy Solicitor-General මහත්මයා කියන්ෙන් එයයි. ෙම්ක තුළින් තමයි අප ෙම් ෙලෝකයට ෙමවැනි අවස්ථාවක් විවෘත කරන්ෙන්. This is the entry. This is the reason why we, in the United National Party have been very vocal with regard to the human rights situation of the country today when day by day people are being abducted in white vans. The judicial system is kept aside. The media freedom is stifled to such an extent that they report only what the Government wants. This is the reason why we have been trying to bring this matter to the notice of the international community. The previous Speaker who spoke from the party that proposed this Motion blackguarded the United States of America. He said that the Government was tempted to sign an agreement. Why did they permit them to carry on with it? They are a part of the Government. They run with the hare and hunt with

the hounds. When they have to go to IPU conferences they go with the Government delegation and when they come back they sit with the Opposition and take the time allocated to the Opposition to speak against the Government. What is this hypocrisy that is going on? That is why I say, "වැඩ බැරි ටාසන්ලා" කියලා. අන්න එතැනයි කියන්ෙන්. අද ජීවන වියදමට උත්තරයක් නැහැ. ෙලෝක බැංකුෙව් "ප්ලග්" එක ගලවලා නැහැ. සිංහරාජය ගැන අසතɕ කිව්වා. ෙම්වාට උත්තර නැතිව තමයි අප ෙම් ගමන් කරන්ෙන්. Again he basically brought the United Kingdom into action. He said that they were helping the Tigers. Then why did His Excellency the President visit Tony Blair when he was enjoying his holidays and say, “Please help us?” Nobody said it. It was not the United National Party, it was not the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe who said it. Because the Ceasefire Agreement was in serious jeopardy he was forced into reality and decided that getting assistance was a better medication rather than taking them to task. Now when they come, they say that they are interfering. In the same way he had a swiping touch on Norway. You came into power saying that you would chase Norway out. Hon. Minister of Foreign Affairs, why are you still keeping Norway? If it is bad, if it is inimical and if the United National Party or the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe has done something wrong, why on earth - you have been three years and four months in Government and one and a half years in Executive Presidency - do you keep Norway? ගරු රවීන්ද සමරවීර මහතා

( மாண்ᾗமிகு ரᾪந்திர சமரᾪர) (The Hon. Ravindra Samaraweera) Norway was brought by them. ගරු රවි කරුණානායක මහතා

( மாண்ᾗமிகு ரவி கᾞணாநாயக்க) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake) Yes. As my good Friend, the Hon. Ravindra Samaraweera says, who brought Norway in? It was ex-President Chandrika Bandaranaike Kumaratunga. At that time we were in Government and because it was brought by the then Opposition or the then President we did not want to go against it. We thought that there was a necessity and that there was a certain good aspect in it. So we took the good points of it and today even after five years and two months it is still going on. The Foreign Minister is running around the world saying, "Yes, we are there to comply with International Covenants; we are there to internationalize international agreements that we have signed". The Hon. Keheliya Rambukwella yesterday in the morning said that there is a necessity for the Ceasefire Agreement. හැබැයි, අද උෙද් කථා කරපු විමල් වීරවංශ මන්තීතුමා කියනවා, ෙම්ක මළ කඳක් ලු; ෙම්ක වළලන්න ඕනෑ ලු. ෙහළ උරුමෙය් ස්වාමීන් වහන්ෙසේලා කියනවා එෙහමම තිෙයනවා ලු. එෙහම නම් ආණ්ඩුෙව් ඉඳ ෙගන ඒ අය ෙමොකට ද ඔක්සිජන් ගහන්ෙන්? ෙම් ෙබොරුවට තමයි අප "වැඩ බැරි

* පුස්තකාලෙය් තබා ඇත. ᾓனிைலயத்தில் ைவக்கப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ. Placed in the Library.

ටාසන්ලා" කියන්ෙන්. ජීවන වියදමට උත්තරයක් නැහැ. සාමයට උත්තරයක් නැහැ. යුද්ධයට උත්තරයක් නැහැ. හැම එකම කරලා, අෙප් අහිංසක ජනතාව අද බිත්තියට තල්ලු කරලා ජාතɕන්තර ෙලෝකෙයන් ඈත් කරන විට තමයි අද එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂය නැඟිටලා අහන්ෙන්, "ෙම් ෙමොනවාද කරන්ෙන්?" කියන එක. නැත්නම් පිට රටවල්වලට අෙප් රටට ඇවිල්ලා අභɕන්තර කටයුතුවලට ඇඟිලි ගහන්න ඉඩ ෙදන්ෙන් නැහැ. නමුත්, අදක්ෂතාව නිසා, වැඩ බැරි ටාසන්ලා නිසා අද රට ෙගනල්ලා තිෙබන්ෙන් ඒ තත්ත්වයට. එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂය ගිහිල්ලා ෙලෝකයාට කියන්න අවශɕයි. අද රෙට් ජන මාධɕයක් නැහැ, බය ෙවලා. ඒ නිසා අප ෙම්ක ෙලෝකයට කියන්න අවශɕයි. ඒ නිසා තමයි අද ෙම් පිටස්තර ෙලෝකය අහන්ෙන් "ෙමොකක්ද ෙම් රෙට් වන්ෙන්?" කියලා. I am asking you the same thing. He took a swipe at India. India is our friend, we have to utilize them. Then he was talking of the British Company, Booker coming and taking land. Why on earth are you giving, you are in Government? So please ensure that you have a consistent policy. I am sure the Government has that - the Opposition definitely has that - but it is the appendages of the Government that do not have this and they are the ones who are creating misery in this country. His Excellency Mahinda Rajapaksa was extended a hand of friendship by the Leader of the Opposition, our Leader of the United National Party. He took it and bit it. Today he finds the sadness of biting it. The momentary thrill of biting has been forgotten and the hunger is growing now. Why on earth did he do it? What has been done is done. Still we are in the international community respecting the sovereignty, the national integrity and the Sri Lankans right to determine their own future. We only go there and tell what is expected. There was a huge debate by the Hon. Anura Priyadharshana Yapa, the Minister of Mass Media and Information trying to entangle the Leader of the Opposition, the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe when he was overseas on what he told the international community. I table* Annex 2. I want it printed in full in Hansard because the general public do not understand what has been told in that. What has been done is a summarization, a collation of twelve letters that have been tabled by the Members of this House, the former Ministers of this House, by the media and by the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe as the Leader of the Opposition on certain matters that have got to be done. I will mention the contents of this Annex. No. 1 - The Memorandum of Understanding between the Sri Lanka Freedom Party and the United National Party on the 23rd of October, 2006. Is there anything

wrong in that? No. 2 - The Statement by the Co-Chairs in November 2006 welcoming the MoU. No. 3 - The Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe’s letter to the President on 27th December 2006 with proposed amendments to the Emergency Regulations and the PTA, Prevention of Terrorism Act. No. 4 - The Statements in Parliament on 6th February about the abrogation of the MoU by the Leader of the Opposition, Mr. Ranil Wickremasinghe. No. 5 - The news reports in “The Sunday Leader’ of 8th April, 2007 on the Statement made by the Hon. Sripathi Sooriyaarachchi on the deal with the LTTE. What is wrong? It was mentioned by the Hon. Sripathi Sooriyaarachchi, an Hon. Member of this House. Of course the Government for saying so has been trying to crucify him but we appreciate the audacity, the sagacity and the honesty because he came out and told the world that this is the actual situation. No. 6 - Complaint to the Chairman of the Commission to Investigate Allegations of Bribery or Corruption by the former Ministers regarding the purchase of MiG 27 dated 14th March 2007. Who are the Ministers? The Hon. Mangala Samaraweera and the Hon. Sripathi Sooriyaarachchi. Did we take them? Did we accompany them? Did we engage them to go and do this? No! They have a feeling for the country. The actual situation is being told by them. So, when the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe as the Leader of the Opposition conveys information which is inimical to the Government, is this something to run down the country? No. 8 - The Statement in Parliament on the 3rd of April, 2007 by the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe regarding the attack on the Katunayake Air Force Base . That is the factual situation which was collated and told in Parliament which was communicated. No. 9 - The Statement on the Breach of Privilege of Parliament on the 20th March, 2007 by the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe. This is what happened to one of the Members, the Hon. Sripathi Sooriyaarachchi when he brought in certain matters that needed to be debated, which is yet to be debated. The Speaker of this House has still to give a ruling on that. No. 10 - The list of 81 names of Tamil persons who disappeared. It is a document by the Civil Monitoring Commission that has been made public and given to the international community. Nobody has disputed it. No. 11 - The letter to the International Press Institute dated 24th April, 2007 by the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe on the continuing deterioration of media freedom in Sri Lanka . This was a request that was made by the media.

So, I as the Secretary handling International Affairs of our party with our Leader, have been trying to do the best of a worse situation that is there. The brief is very bad. When there is a issue in Colombo they call Scotland Yard. Now, Scotland Yard is not in North Korea, not in Cuba, not in Zimbabwe. They come from Britain. එතැනදී බිතානɕෙයන් එන ෙකොට පශ්නයක් නැහැ. ෙම් වැඩ බැරි ටාසන්ලා ඔය ජාතɕන්තර ෙලෝකයට බැණලා හරි යන්ෙන් නැහැ. අෙප් රෙට් බඩගින්න අප විසඳන්න අවශɕයි. අෙප් රෙට් යටිතල පහසුකම් දියුණු කරන්න අවශɕයි. අෙප් රෙට් මානව අයිතිවාසිකම්වලට අපි උත්තරයක් ෙදන්න අවශɕයි. අෙප් රෙට් ජනමාධɕ භය කරනවා නම් ඒකට නිර්භීතව උත්තරයක් දීම අෙප් යුතුකමක්. ඒක කරන්න යන ෙකොට තමයි අනුර යාපා ඇමතිතුමා ගිහින් කියන්ෙන්, "රනිල් විකමසිංහ රට පාවා ෙදනවා"යි කියා. ෙම්වා ද පාවා ෙදන්ෙන්? පාවා ෙදන්ෙන් තමාලෙග් කටයුතු තුළින් තමයි. [බාධා කිරීමක්] ඔව්. ඔබතුමාලට කියන්න පුළුවන්. පච කියන රූපවාහිනියක් තිෙබනවා. අසතɕ කියන "සිළුමිණ" ක්, "දිනමිණ" ක් තිෙබනවා. ඊට පස්ෙසේ ඕෙක ගිහින් ඉන්නවා. ඕක මහ ෙලොකු ෙදයක් යැ? ඉතින් ඔන්න ඔය වාෙග් ෙදයකට, අපි කියපු එකට උත්තරයක් තිෙබනවා ද? The Government appointed the Civil Monitoring Committee and people started reporting to it about missing people. Likewise is the Committee of Eminent Persons. Who invited them? Mr. Mahinda Samarasinghe called them and said "Please, come to our country". Because obviously they were fighting a situation that was very difficult for them to grapple with in Colombo.
